sorer dyd soo leye cryynge yt grete pyte thenne came monke hym asked hym done syknes come ayen sayd nothynge thenne said monke thou shriuen sith thou hole sayde nay noo nede stale nother oxe cowe dyd noo gryuous synne thenne monke thoughte thoughe man doo noo dedely synne maye doo many venyall maye make dedely synne ryghte man may wyth many smale cornes charge stronge horse soo maye lade soule wyth soo many smale sinnes maye falle pytte helle thenne anone man wente preeste shroue hym soo hole bothe body soule euer confessio preyers holy virgyne amen pdominica iiii quadragesie ood men wymmen fourthe sonday lenton whiche holy chirche maketh mencion holy prophete called moyses whiche fygure lorde ihesu criste many yeres lorde borne thenne rede holy chirche moyses deserte synay god spake hym sayd pvidi afflictione populi mei qui est egipto clamorem eius audiui c ppharao kynge egypte oppresseth soo peple israel wyth bondage vnresonable werkes woo cryde socoure helpe wherfore goo thou thyder brynge hem oute bondage shall wyth thenne bryng hem offre hem wyll brynge hem londe plentuousnes goodis soo whan taught moyses sholde doo moyses went thyder gadered tholde peple gyder knewe prophecye shold ladde oute londe sayde hem god bad hym thenne full glade wente wyth hym olde yonge tyll came rede see god euyr byfore hem daye pyler cloude refresshe hem fro hete sonne nyghte pyler fyre lyghte hem fro harme venym beestis whan pharao herde moyses hadde forth people toke thre hondred char ottis owne thre hondred londe xl thousande horsmen thre hondred thousande fote men went whan moyses sawe peple come prayed god helpe god hym selfe bad hym smyte see wyth yerde et percussit mari rubro whan smytten see way hym people see cloue two partyes soo water stode stylle euery syde hyll grounde eye sonde thenne moyses yede forthe people hym thenne wende pharao haue passed also sewed ofte wha oste wythin see water went gyder drowned hym oste whan moyses sawe yt peple peryshed thus thanked god vii dayes euery day yede see thankinge god passage makynge great melodye lord done soo yet mynde herof ester weke make solempne procession fonte rede see pthenne wente moyses forthe wyth people deserte tylle came hylle synay lefte peple benethe stabat moyses super monte pand moyses stode vpon hyll god xl dayes xl nyghtes wythoute mete drynke pthenne god gaue hym two table stone whiche god wrote wyth owne fyngres ten commaundementes toke theym moyses pand bad hym teche hem people whan moyses came downe peple face bryghte sonne two spite stondyng hede lyke two horne soo people myght speke wyth hym clerenes abscondit moyses faciem sua pthenne moyses hyde face wyth kerchiff thenne one leef wryten thre comaundemetes longen god ben thyse pthe first thou shalt worshippe thy god loue hym aboue thinge thou shall directe maner thynge goddis wyll byfore thyne owne sue thyn owne wylle pthe seconde co maundemente thou shalt take name veyne saye thou shall bee called goddis childe crysten man fende thenne name vayn palso thou shall swere god noo parte body noo thynge made forderynge trouthe yet whan thou arte constreyned therto pthe thirde commaundemente thou shall kepe thyne holy daye saye thou shall erly vp late downe serue god holy daye thou arte werkedaye thyne owne werke besy shall thou hooly daye serue god pthe fourthe commaundemente thou shall worshippe thy fader thi moder yt brought worlde also thy godfader thy godmoder yt made crysten man thy fader vnder god hath cure charge thy soule pthe fyfthe thou shall sle man nother wyth tonge wyth thy honde wyth euyll ensample sixte thou shall stele mannes godes vii thou shalt doo lechery viii thou shall bere noo false wytnesse nynthe thou shall nat coueyte thy nyghboures godes ne thing longeth ayenst wyll tenthe thou shall nat desire thy neyghboures wyf ne cou seyll noo waye euyll sholde harme vilonye husbonge thies x comaundmentes whiche euery cristen man woman bonde kepe thus moyses figure token criste moyses camme bifore yaue lawe criste came gaaf grace mercy pfor maner moyses fette people oute egypte thrughe rede see forth hylle sinay wyse crist whan came prechynge myracles doyng fette people dernesse synne euyl lyuyng thorugh water baptysme hylle vertuous lyuyng pand therfore wyll shryue hym clene leue fowle lyuing kepe commaundementis god made couenaunte kepe cristning thene shal encreased hygher tha ony hyl erth yt heuen wyll thus muste fedde wyth fyue loues two fysshes pwe rede daye holy chirche gospell criste fedde fyue thousand people wyth fyue looues two fysshes fyrste loff fyue contricion synne seconde shryfte mouth thirde satisfaction trespasse pthe fourth tourne ayen synne ofte aferde shall doo well fyfthe perseueraunce good lyuynge two fysshes ben good orysons almesdedes thyse norysshed water wepynge teres deuocion thyse two fysshes geten god wylle pnarracio pit wreten somtyme man called pyers ryche man soo harde noo begger myght gete hym thenne tyme happed many beggers satte gyder place spake pyers myghte gete noo good hym pthenne spake one theym mayster sayde wylle ye ley wyth shall gete noo good hym soo made wager thenne wente man forth came pyers place set hym doune porche halle dore abode tyll pyers came anone sawe pyers spake soo horryble pyers grete angre seruauntes came hym wyth basket brede toke loof wyth myghte caste atte beggers hede smote hym brest sayd stoppe thy mouth wyth deuylle stoppe anone begger caught loofe ranne waye felowes shewed loof soo gate wager pthenne next nyghte happed soo pyers shryuen brought bedde soo deyed anone fendes came take soule thenne lady redy bad brynge sowle soo dyde thenne noo thynge helpe soule lof cast begger thenne sayde fendys gaaf ayenste wylle therfore ryght sholde helpe hym pthenne wente oure lady sone prayenge hym graunte soule goo body ayent loke yf pwolde amende thenne lorde badde vere soule ayen body whan soule wyth body anone satte vp gaaf great syghynge called hym seruauntes tolde hem hard dome dampned hadde lof cast begger ptherfore anone made selle good deled poure people fore goddis sake whan hadde done soo made hym selfe heremyte holy man phere ye maye well wyte grete almesdede preyers made man preuy wyth god soo syker ayenst dome pfor haue done almysdede goddis sake shall bee saued yf oute dedely synne pwe fynde vowtry man take another mannys wyfe woman another husbonde greuous sinne ye shall ensample pnarracio somtyme man made charcoles wode whan made grete fyre leye therby nyght soo aboute mydnyght came woman rennynge afore man blacke horse faste myght ryde hunted abowte wyth naked swerde aboute fyre last man slewe woman hew peces cast fyre rode ayen wyth myght soo whan man sawe done many nyghtes thenne went lord told hym mater thenne lorde bolde knyght sai wyte mente thyder nyght fonde man tolde thenne knyght asked spiryte dyde thenne saide suche man told name seruaunt lytyll sore woman ther knyghtes wif haddeley husbondes lyf therfore bothe put penaunce sayde horse ryde fende yt brenneth c fold worse ony fyre myghte erthe peyne muste suffre tyl helpe good preyers mass almes dedes tolde hym many thynges knyghte dyde alle thinges sayd shold helpe delyuered hem oute peyne euerlastyng blysse god brynge v amen pdominica passione dni good men wymmen daye called sondaye passion weke daye oure lord ihesu criste began passion iewes suche enuye cause tolde defautes ce mysliuyng soo cause repreued hym soo daye full assented hym deth soo aboute ofte byfore letted thynge fere comen people helde hym prophete pbut daye uytte hem togider fully accorded wolde spa noo thynge sholde dede wherfore gospell tellith criste prechyd temple iewys rebuked spytously sayd nunc cognouimus quia demonium habes nowe knowe thou haste fende tempte haue made speke som euyl worde whiche mighte haue putt repreefe tolde goddes sone redy haue stoned deth knewe well ther malice iesus autem abscondit se et exiuit de templo iesus hyd selue went oute temple pthus oure lord day began passion wherfore holy churche redeth weke booke ierom prophete firste prophyced cristes passion tolde howe maner iewys sholde doo hym dethe thenne ye shall vnderstonde wele wyse iewys pursuyd criste deth wyse fere gretly lest moche false people cristned pursuen criste heuyn nowe psainte austyn sayth synne greuously pursue heuyn iewys dyd pursued erth thenne ye wol wete whiche take hede criste marked sayd thus oui ex deo est verba dei audit god heryth worde god heryth nat word god sweryth many grete othes ful falsely thi tho heuyn glade whan haue foule dede doon grounded foule cursed lyuynge synne w nat amende theym prechinge techynge euir foull dedes anone redy fyghte chyde tell h defautes shewyd crist harme condiciones people suche nowe dayes shall haue many enmyes wyll saye trouthe may preue ensample pnarracio pthere somtyme mawmente cyte wold tell thinge stole myssed hadde hpped tyme yt yonge man hadde stole thinge aferde mawmente anone went mawmet fayde thus well wote thou mayste de grete shame velonye god beleue vpon thou discouer wyll breke thy bede soo went forth waye thenne soone came missed gode praynge mawmente tell criste suffred passion openly hadde hanging vpon croce saynge consummatum est endyd yt saye prophecy passion hath end wherfore clothes myn autre ben take away cristes clothes wer take fro doon naked croce saue oure ladye modre wounde kirchef couer mebres auter stone betokeneth crystis body drawen crosse skyn parchement harowe soo bonys myghte tolde pthe besomes aulter wasshen betokeneth scourge bete oure lordes body wyth thornes crowned wyth water wyne wasshen wyth betokeneth blode water ronne downe woundis syde perished wyth spere wyne poored vpon aulter fyue cross betokeneth blode ranne downe pryncypall woundes body palso daye noo pax gyuen masse iudas betrayed cryste nyghte wyth cosse thus prophecye passion daye ended wherfore nyghte whan hadde souped made sacramete owne body gaue synnes thenne yf people aske preestes masse souper cryste dyde tourned honeste saluacion mannys soule haymo telleth vpon pystle saynt poule many begynnynge feyth come chirche thursdaye riche brought mete drynke wyth hem eten dranke ner belyes full thenne night en housell sayd criste gaue hem ensample whan riche ete dranke moche poure people abeydeth wythoute tyll ryche hath doone sore hungred thenne ete releef lefte soo peple toke housell pystell daye telleth psaynt poule rebuketh hem therof tourneth foule vse honest clennes holynesse saye masse fastyng people take housell fastyng ester byheft iherusalem soo passed sauf founde soo vii dayes come vnto see thanked god passage mynde herof holy chirche vseth ester weke goo procession fo e nowe rede see cristen people ben crystened fonte water fonte betokenethe rede see blode water wounde cristis syde power pharao sede helle drowned al might lost cristen peple saued fo te halowed ester euen wytson euyn begynnyng al child abode cristened vnto thyse two dayes crystened atte fonte halowynge cause many soo longe abydyng dede wythout crystendome therfore holy chirche ordeyned nowe cristen tymes yere saue viii dayes byfore thise euyns child shal abyde fonte halowyng yf maye perryll deth ellys pthus pascall halowed lyghte wyth newe fyre al tapres candellis ben lyghte holynesse good techynge good liuing cometh crist teching holy chirche lighteth hem crist passion wyth brennynge loue charyte peces enfence ben stycked pascall maner crosse betoke fyue woundes lorde bede sayth suffred body shall fresshe swe ony ensence tyll daye dom greate repreef shall bee dampned belyue crystis passion wyll aske mercy fo yeuenesse synnes fonte halowyng prest casted water foure partyes fonte cryste hadde disciple goyng prechynge techyng foure party cristendom name fader sone holy goost prest bretheth water holy gooste makynge worlde borne vpon water pfor whan god adamis synne cursed therthe londe cursed water wherfor lawfull man ete lenton cometh water droppeth wex water candell brennynge whiche betokeneth manhode crist fullyd water putteth oyle creme water vertu sacrament ben heuen erthe ben ioyned gyder preued crystis baptisme fader heuen spake sayde hic est filius meus dilectus quo michi bene complacui well beloued sone yt wyll pleyse holy ghost seen sicut columba whyte doue thus fonte halowed two tymes yere patt wythsontyde ester whan people broughte oute thraldom crystis passion fro dangeour fende wytsontide thenne holy ghoste yeuen remyssion synnes pthenne fonte people goon quere syngyng letanye prayenge sayntes heuene praye god gyue crysten kepe sacrament goddis pleysaunce couenaunt yt haue made crystenyng thenne preest goth masse cryste hede holy chirche rysen kyrieleyson said euery prayer especyall masse grete nede aske helpe socoure god kepe v maner temptacion fende putteth v namely goddis seruice gloria excelsis said fader heue hath gret ioye holde peple sone hath boughte wyth passion see hem reste pea charyte echone wyth greyle sayd ben newe cristened yet parfyte walke grace vertues alleluya said gre ioye angellis see crystenynge nombre hem restored ayen alleluya tracte said hyghe songen though crystenynge wasshe synne yet muste traueyle besely kepe hem comberaunce fende falle dedely synne offertorye said wymmen comen wyth oynementis offre crystis body fonde hym tombe agnus dei said noo pax gyuen cryste hede pea rysen postcomyn sayde ben newe crystened shold housled daye morowe olde tyme come crystenynge peple grete age thenne short euynsonge done child cristned wherof gretly noyed wyth seknesse colde longe seruyce thenne ended vnder shorte colet sacramente cristenyng ended passion crist whiche cristen people restored tor euerlastyng blisse whiche god brynge v amen pin die paraceues good frendis daye called good frydaye oure lord ihesu cryste suffred daye tourned v grete ioye daye suffred passion vnder pounce pylate oure sake olde sawe yt foule begnnnynge hathe fowle endyng nowe see howe pylate began cursedly ended full wretchedly saynt austyn saith cursed lyuyng first asketh cursyd ende forgeteth hym self lyuyng full lyke forgete hym selfe last ende pylate knyghtes sone called tyrus gate hym woman hyghte pyle womannys fader hyghte atte whan childe borne sette moders name grande fader soo bothe name called hym pylat pthenne whan thre yeres age moder brought hym kynges courte thenne hadde knyghte another sone nygh lyke pylates age knightes sone rule gentyler manfully goodly beloued pylate soo hate enuye therof pylate slewe knyghtes sone thenne knyghte wonder sory yet wolde slee pylate sente hym rome hostage trybut knyght sholde paye themperour pthenne happed kynge fraunce hadde sent sone theder cause thenne cause pwhan pylate sawe beloued chereshed therfore pylate slewe hym ne cursed themperoure counseyll romayns sente pylate contree yt called pounce people contrey cursed slewe ony come bee thyr mayster ouer hem soo whan pylate come thyder applied hym maners soo wyth whyles sotyltye ouercome hem maystrye gate name called pylate po ce grete domynacion power thenne kynge iherusalem sent made lyeuftenaunt vnder hym londe iury pylate lyked well office preuely sente themperour offyce confermed hym vnwetynge kynge herode kynge tyme wherfore whan kynge herode herde hadde done soo wrothe enmyes vnto tyme oure lorde ihesu crist take thenne become frendis ayen fylle bothe one aset cristis deth thenne happed afterward themperour fylle syke sent criste hele hym tolde hym cryste heled tho euer wolde come hym maner sykenesse soo euer sykenesse soo bee thenne pylate done hym deth messager come thenne whan themperoure vnderstode sent pylate made hym come hym pand whan pylate herde sore aferd take cristis cote soo whan come rome themperour presece made pilate good chere whyle cristis te themperour swore byfore shold ded thenne toke cote anone cote themperour sore wrothe wythe pylate putte hym pryso tyll take counseyll dethe shold deye thenne soone pylate wist vnderstod sholde dede toke owne knyfe slewe hym self wyth whan emperour herde therof vnderstode sleyn hym self thenne anone made bynde grete stone aboute pylats longe tyme water many horryble syghtes seen aboute cursed man thus oure lorde ihesu cryste suffred passion dethe mankynde fyrst whan take dyde buffete hym stryped hym naked bete hym wyth scourgis pa vertice capitis v que ad plantas pedumnon fuit eo sanitas pthat hyest place hede sole fete noo thynge lefte hole hym raw made crowne thornes set hede bete doune wyth stauis reede perisshed brayne whan aungell ioachim saide wordes badde ioachim take lambe offre sacrifice god soo dyd whan fro mydday euensong tyme ley gro de prayer thankynge god al hert thene morow aungell badde wente homwarde anne wyf shepe whan came nygh home aungell came anne badde goo yate called golden yate abyde husbonde tyll come thenne glad toke maydynes went gate mette ioachim said lord thanke wedowe wyf barrayn nowe shall bere childe wo wepinge nowe shall ioye likynge soone anne conceyued oure lady whan borne called mary au gell badde bifore thanne yt wenyd brought te ple lefte emong virgynes serue god bothe yt hadde gadred moche good lordes gadred went bere lothe thenne ther theuys sette robbe hym waye wode muste nedes goo soo whanne come wode bethoughte hym yt hadde saide lady saulter wonte knelyd doune began saye come lady lyke fair mayden set garlonde hede eche aue maria sette rose garlond soo brighte woode shone therof whan done kyssed erthe wente waye thenne come theues toke hym ladde hym mayster whiche seen thyse doynges thenne sayd hym woman yt set garlonde hede sayd syre sothe see ne woman ne garlonde thenne sayde mayster thefe wote well thou arte lordys man hast moche good wyth wolde fayn wyte woma come thou knelest downe sayd wha see aferde also bethoughte hadde sayde oure lady faulter kneled doune say prayng lady helpe nede thenne sayd loue goo thy waye praye v soo went waye sauf thenne anone te peste ceased well sayled forth thabbot dyd message come ayen sauf sou de spedde well euery degre whan come home tolde kyng vision kyng made hym preche reame aboute thus alowed holy haue hym helle thenne come lady sayd hast thou take man fende sayde fynde hym seruyce goyng avowtry thenne sayd lady seruice anone restored hym lyf ayen bad hym synne bad hym halow concepcion soo dyde thomas hadde doon anone cryed sayd grete wondre dominus meus et deus meus lorde god beleue yt thou arte god man lorde saide thus bti qui crediderut viderut blessed beleue se nat thou haste seen thou byleueste yet taryenge thomas brought v fadder beleue blessinge oure iesu criste speketh sainte gregory sayth thomas ynde thou haste holpe fayth woldest nat beleue tyll thou haddest felyd woundes thenne mary mawdeleyn dyd beleue firste sighte minus est enim maria magdalena que cicius credidit qua thomas qui diu dubitauit thus thomas preuyd oure feyth beleue nede neuir varye ne doubte palso tombe euer laye wythout also prechyng techyng taught duodecim gradus virtutum assignare primus est vt deum crederent qui est vnus essencia et trinus personis dedit eis triplex exemplum sensibile quomodo sint diuidenci vna tres persone primum e quia vnum est homine sapiencia et de vna procedit intellectus memoria et genium memoria est vt non obliuiscaris intellectum vt intelligas que ostendi possunt veldoceri ingenium e vt quod didiceris inuenias secundum est quia vna vinea tria sunt lignum folium et fructus et hec omnia tria sunt vinea tercium e quia capud nostrum e quatuor sensibus constat vno autem capite sunt visus auditus adoratus et gustus et hec plura sunt et tamen vnum capud secundus gradus est vt baptismum suscipiat tercius gradus est vt fornicatione abstineat quartus vt well dryngeth body full water right iohn drank soule full gostly wisedome atte cristes brest tyme lorde shewyd preuyte bifore olde wolde nat leue preche worde god emperoure exiled iohn selfe alone yle hym childe shepe ete fere lest wolde haue come cyte thenne whan chyldren shepe nye ete cause yt kyng hym self gaue counseyll constreyned hym doughter gyue dragon thenne kynge fere people wyth wepyng grete sorowe makynge delyuered hem childe sente forth place ere wont set child shepe wyth abyde tyll dragon come ordynaunce god saynt george come tydyng waye whan sawe damoysell araye thought woman greate byrth asked stode therre wyth ye shepe suche araye mornynge thenne answered said gentyll knyght well maye morne make sorowe kynges doughter cite sette deuoured dragon hath ete chyldren cite dystroyed nowe muste haue fader gaf hem counseyll therto therfore gentyll knyght ryde hense faste saue thy selfe leest dragon sle bothe thenne sayd george damoysell grete shame vylonye knyghte well arayed shold fle thou woman sholdest abyde thene wyth yt dragon put oute hede hole spytted fyre proferd batayle george made sygne crosse hym sett spere reste wyth grete myght bare downe dragon grounde thenne bad damoysell bynde dragon wyth gyrdell necke lede wyth cite soo dragon folowed hadde honde maide bowe paciently whan people cyte sawe dragon come fledde fere awaye thenne george called peple co passyon sory pour ony dysease thenne whan george done thus torned al londe crysten feyth herde emperour hyght dyoclesian dyde many craste men deth thenne wente hym rebuked hym cursed thenne emperour commaunded put george anone pryson laye hym vpryght lay mylstone vpon breest presse hym deth thenne george prayed god helpe lady kepte hym yt hadde noo harme parte body whan emperour herde therof dyde make two wheles put hem full hokes george sette myddes bytwene thenne wheles tourned soo rase flesshe fro bone whan george tou ment anone prayed god socour helpe anone holpe thenne put hym hote limekylle closed hym ther shold haue brente oure lorde tourned colde iii dayes thenne wente haue founde hym brente sauff fro maner harmes mery thenne brought forth set byfore emperour george repre ed hym fals goddis said hym fendes wythout myght power thenne emperour made bete mouth wyth stone tyll powned made bete bare body wyth drye besomes tyll flesshe fyll bone people myghte see guttes yet made hym drynke venym made strong none haue payned hym deth whan george made signe crosse dranke poyson wythout greeff moche man made poyson tourned cristen feyth anone done deth pthenne nyght george pryson god come hym sayd george good comforte morowe thou shalt make ende come euerlastynge ioye blysse set crowne hede gaff hym blessynge thenne morowe wolde doo worship false goddis goost wente cyte alisaunder torne people feyth thenne wha come cite vnnethe entred cite shoo brast therby wyft well shold dede thenne sawe man sytte clout shone poure peple marke prayed hym mende shoo thenne man pour hym thoughte almesse helpe hym yt tyme toke shoo began sewe anone wyth nalle hurte honde ache grete payne said god helpe wha marke herde called god anone marke prayed god hym thenne marke spytted erth blyssed anoynted hode therwyth sayd nomine patris ihesu cristi filii dei viui sanctur man tu name fader ihesu cryste sone quycke god thy honde hol pvocabatur autem homo ille ananias forsoth man called ananya whan ananya sawe suche vertu marke prayed hym dwelle styl wyth hym comoratus que ibidem duobus annis dwelled two yeres cristened hym al houshold afterwarde grete holynesse marke sawe man made hym arshebysshop thenne people sawe marke preched cite toke hym teyed rope aboute necke drewe hym amonge stone tyll flesshe fell erthe sayd drawe bugull bugull place soo whan drawe nye deth thenne putte hym pryson tyll morowe thenne nyghte cryste come hym pryson sayde pea marke myn euangelyste agast wyth thenne morowe come fett oute pryson drewe hym tyll dede whan sholde dye sayde manus tuas soo gaue vp gooste pand afterwarde wolde bre e body thenne came suche erth quake wyth lyghtenynge thonderyng yt ther durst man abide thenne nyght crysten people come toke markis body beryed thenne felle euery cristen lo de halowed saint markis day saue one countrey called appolonya whiche countrey greued wyth hete droughte countrei fayled theym frute well nye famysshed come voys heuen bad theim halowe saynt markis daye thene shold comforted dede soo anone god sent hem plente maner frutes ynough pnow wyte sholde faste daye goo procession rede cyte rome daye fell suche qualme soden deth whan man yaned gaped f esed anone deyed deyed many sodeynly thenne pope called pellagius comaunded cristen people whan yaned euery man shold make crosse ouer mouthe whan ony man herd another f ese shold saye crist helpe soo many saned made people goo procession prayed sayntes heuen praye god soo dyde thenne come saynt gregori made doo saynt markis day halowe fast goo procession canonysed done euer thenne come pope called liberius tyme maner frutes tyme yere grete tendernesse self toke grete harme soo thonder lightenyng vnkynde hetes stormes myldewes wormes longe taylde flyes greate vengeaunce yt anone ester daye people iourned ayen olde synne hauyng rewarde sacrament whiche haue receyued thrfore god sente vengeaunce tyme tha ony tyme yere wherfore holy pope put awaye thyse thinges especyall goddis wreche fro people commaunded cristen people halowe fast goo procession sayd yt made constytucion acursed tyll come amendement therfore charge counseyll al thynke saued hem suche sykenesse woo sorowe yt cryed helpe thene said philipe hem yf ye wold holpen heled siknesse also thyse men rered deth lyfe fyrste cast doune mametes set theyr stede cross lord deyed vpon doo worship thenne dyde glad holpen sikenesse assone hadde doo soo holpen thenne philyppe prayed god thyse thre men reyse deth lyf tunc precepit philippus dracom vt locum suum redescenderet pthenne phylyppe commaunded dragon goo downe place aye neuer disease man thenne cursed peple cyte sawe phylyp wolde haue tourned people toke hym dyde hym vpon crosse soo crosse deyed wente euerlastyng blisse pnow shall ye iacob called amonge appostles iacobus minor lesse iames knewe iacobus maior iames saynt iohan euangelist brother whan iacobus iames one name called cristis owne brother soo moche lyke maner drynke myght make man dronke ne neuer ete flesshe ne hede neuer shauen ne vsed neuer baumed wyth oyle maner countrey hete sonne ware neuer lynen clothe lay vpon knee prayeng people knee soo thyk worlde neuir lyke haue wonne sone distroyed vnto vttermoost somoche yt stone walles cyte turned vp side doune lord iesu criste sayd xl wynter bifore yt shulde soo iewes dryuen oute diuerse contrees wolde haue take vengeance cytee hapnyd man pylates whiche dyd crist deth came fro ierusalem towarde rome tempest see toke droue vpon lande temple gret te peste duelled grete lorde yt called vaspasian cause called soo malady nose threlles dropped oute nose wormes lyke waspes saide vaspasian man fro countrey comest thou aunswered saide fro ierusalem wolde towarde rome saide vaspasian gladde therof haue herd say many grete lech countre wherfore wolde well thou coudest hele thou doo nat hele thou shall dede aunsweryd said leche selue lyth seke reyseth dede lyue may hele wyl saide vaspasian sir said iesu nazereth iewes slewe thou wyl beleue thou shalte haue thou wyll desyre hole said vaspasian beleue verily thou saifte maye hele reyseth men dethe lyf anon worde hole gladde hole anoon sente ayen rome lefte tytus sone distroye cyte tytus laye sore cyte famysshed theym somoche ete shone botes fader tooke mete fro sone sone fader either toke others mouth husbond fro wyf wyf fro husbonde emonge woman grete birthe come gentyll bloodde haddde yonge childe hungre sayd dere child haue suffred peyne tha euyr thou dedyste wherfore reason ease hungre thanne though dyed thou also toke childe slewe rosiyd halue kepte half tyll morowe flesshe rosiyd sauour went cytee whanne people felte sauoure wened hadde ple tye mete come haue part thene woman wold haue hid saide wolde see whatt mete mediatoure bitwene god theym may haue repentaunce theire hertes shryfte mouthe satisfactyon dede doyng may come blisse neuir shall haue ending amen de inuencione sancte crucis goode frendes suche daye ye shall haue inuencion holy crosse ye shall nat faste euyn come god holye churche cristen people shulde doo worshyp yt dyed crosse thenne ye shall vnderstond called thus inuencio sancte crucis thyse two saintes yt holy appostles praye v oure lord hath peter one syde poule ye syde hath woundes open fresshe bledyng shewing maner cristen people suffred woundes v bee v welles mercy suffred v pye shall vnderstonde yt thyse two appostles first grete synners left synne sory contryte synned nomore lord toke hem ensample wyl leue synne shal saued shreuen forsaketh synne mercy foloweth yt doo penaunce shall haue meercy grace glad fader see sonne rise deth lyfe also glad lord moche gladder see man rise oute dedely synne neuer doo therfore shewyng ensample poule bereth swerde cristen people cut awaye cheynes synne wyth sharpe swerde confession dedely synne byndeth man sore fende therfore cut awaye cheyne peter also redy open gate heuen cristen people take wyll forsake synne pye shall vnderstonde ye poule first soo hye soo feerse ayenst al goddis seruautes yt durst precher deale wyth hym lefte grete malice ferse gracious hye proud herte meke lowly goddis seruautes peter also held hym self perfyte stedfast cristis dyscyples wherfore made bost vayn glory redy goo dethe wyth cryst sayd thus behoueth deye wyth whan cryste sey discyples shold forsake hym peter grete bost sayd though men forsake hym wold yet ouer whan criste take peter drewe oute swerd smote seruauntes ere hyghte malcus soone whan sawe crist take shold put deth thenne swered stared yt neuer knewe hym forsoke crist whan herde kocke crowe thenne remembred lord sayd hym kocke crewe iii thou shalte forsake thenne peter went forth et fleuit amare wept bytterly hyd hym caue durst come among bredren shame tyll oure lord sente hym name thenne peter euer ashamed sory trespas boster vnstable wordes afterwarde trewe stable grounded stablenesse parfyght lyuyng soo moche yt crist called hym peter yt stone englisshe thou layest stone thou shalt fynde soo peter soo stedfast nether wele woo neuer flitered euer stode stedfast cristis lawe euer synne mynde amende amysse afterwarde grete abstynence ete brede oyle wortes full selden flesshe wered syngyll kertyll mantell euer often herde ony man mynde ihesus anone began wepe ful sore whan herde ony kocke crowe anone wold ryse vp goo praye suffre forth gyder preched thenne many wrothe peter tourned soo moche people ferth put hym pryson bonde hym fast wyth grete cheynes yron tyll nye dede leste soold bee stolen awaye wherfore knyghtes woke shold escape thus comyn people toke ensample hem make fyres worshippe saynt peter watche thenne criste come peter pryso thenne come angell peter wyth grete lyghte lorde badde anone cheynes breke fyll fro hondes fete soo wente rome pope xxxv yeres tourned moche people cristis feythe soone came fendes lymme called symo magus yt cowde moche fendes crafte made moche people lyke dyuerse sykenesse blynde lame deff peple fere wonder byleued hym thenne peter heled symon magus hadde buried bad shold byleue hym thenne symon magus wroth wyth peter myghte haue wyll especyall myghte reyse dede body lyfe peter reysed thenne symon teyed fende lykenesse grete dogge peter sholde come sle peter ppeter sed hym lete dogge lose thenne lepte symon pulled hym doune vnder fete thenne peter bad leue hym noo harme body rente clothes symon wente almost naked awaye thenne symon ordeyned wayes cowde haue peter dede thenne lord appered peter sayde psimon et nero contra te cogitant symonde nero haue ordeyned thy deth morowe wyll sende poule seruaunt comforte ye shall suffre marterdom gyder sake soo come euerlastynge blysse thenne peter tolde bretheren vysion nyght soo toke clemente honde set hym chayer anone peter said comaunde angelis sathanas yt ye lete man goo doune al peple may see thei haue worshyped thenne symond felle doune brast thene themperour wroth made lede peter poul forth dyde peter called hermogynes discyple hyghte phylyp two begyled soo people iames hadde torned ayen mawmetry thenne iames blamed hem torne fro euerlastyng saluacio euerlastyng dampnacion thenne hermogynes herde therof came disputed wyth me feyth hopyng wyth th dis crafte haue ouer come hym thenne iames dyde soo many myracles phylyp forsoke hermogynes mayster thenne hermogynes wroth sent company fendes saide go ye bringe iames phylip bounde thenne whan fe de come iames aungell god redy bond fendes thei cryed iames appostyll haue mercy v bound sore wyth brennynge cheynes wo v euery syde saide iames wherfore ye come hyder said hermogynes sente v hyder brynge philyp bound goddes angelles haue bound v yt wo v suffre peyne thenne sayd iames wyll louse ye go hermogines bringe hyder bou de doo harme thenne saide hermogines thou haste sente v haue boud yron cheynes nowe wyll bynde bringe bifore iames saide iames false hermogynes hath doo v moche tribulacion disease nowe gyue v leue venge v thenne treasoure holy churche pore people hadde nede thenne decius made slee philyps sone fere left wolde auenge faders deth whanne hadde come mannys state tresoure pope sixtus laurence hadde tresoure put firste rotyd thyne herte sholde braunche synne brek oute therof thus lucifer fayrest aungell heuyn made foulest deuyll hell also chore datan abyron felaushyp rose agaynst moises aron grete pryde therfore erthe opnyd swalowed hem quycke downe hell also peple nynyue grete boldnes pryde hadde turne ayen synne hundred score thousand people byble e yth destroyed bodily enemyes therfore euery man beware syn wysely loke myrrour mekenesse techyth hym shalbe first considre thou made foul stynkynge slyme fylth synne lecherye borne thy modre grete sorowe payne norisshed grete laboure angre kepte grete drede nowe thou arte lak foule dunge swetnesse ne frute comyth tree leuys cometh floures frute lyce nyttes fleen herbes also comethe swete smelles aboue benethe party stynkynge fylthe thyn ende thou shall wormes mete turne agayn erthe tyll day dome thy body soule shall ryse agayne gyddre day saythe malachy shall brenne hote furneys fyre proude men shall stoble whiche shalbe bret shall nother rote ne r nd therfore saith isodre mekenes make thy selue leest lowest stretche nat forth thy wynges pryde boost enhansyng thy self lesse thou settyst thy selue sayth god settyth shamefaste chere dismayde loke proudely shame syn walke alowe chere meke mode sadde vysage high worshyppe haue grete mekenesse higher yt thou arte meker thou sholdest make thy self thynke howe oure souerayne lorde iesu mekyd self deth thy sake thus mekenesse vtter remedy agaynste pryde sauatyf salue maner myscheuys synne maketh haue mynde thy shorte abydynge strayte dome thou shalte come thy mekenes thou sholdest haue hadde seconde synne enuye whan thou arte sory thy neighboures welfare ioyest euyll fare wycked synne comyth many braunches one hateryd whanne thou arte lothe speke spoken thynge whiche myght turne thy neyghboure good nother fals demynge dedes thridde bacbytynge speke euyll behynde thou mayst nat ne wylte nat anome fore though thou spekest nat euyll thy self thou hast lykynge euyl spekynge soo thou synnest dedely nat onely speketh euyll also woll gladly euyl spoken defaute synne herer ther bacbytynge ne bacbyter therfore sayth isodre nat glad fall euyll fare thy neyghboure lest god turne wrathe fro hym thou sholdest fall worse glade sorow deseased euirmore morne mischeyf thou wold thyn owne loue peace outwarde inward peace men make pea hate flee chydynge ware awaye occasion stryfe lyue alwaye pea let nothynge passe thy lyppes may defoul cry herers vayn worde take vayne consciece suche word suche soull therfore besy nat speke lyketh yt nedyth take hede thou spekest thou spekyst nat bothe spekynge nat spekynge right well ware thou mayst nat call agayn thou haste saide put fro thy tung synne bacbytynge defoull nat thy mouthe nother mannes synne thou bacbytest nother drede thy self whanne thou blamest nother thynke thyne owne synne loke nat mennys thou shalt neuyr bacbyte thou wylt beholde thy selue therfore ne lysten noo suche tytulers lyke gyltye herer bakbyter desyre nat wyt ye parteynethe nat ask neuir dothe speketh sayth leue ye perteynethe nat greate besynesse amende thyn owne synne asmoche thou beholdest mennys noman knoweth whether worthy hate mede say payne ioye many semeth v right good yet agaynst god happely right nought many one also seme v right noughte yet right dere therfore noman deme put iugement god thus charite knotte vertues thou must distroye foull synne enuye thus charite stondeth loue god loue thy neyghboure whyche ii lawe god abydeth one may nat louyd withoute ye thou loue god thou wy te noon haue ne thou wylt nat take name vayne ne brecke thyn holy day thou loue thy neighboure thou wylt manslaughter ne thyfte ne false wytnes bere ne lichery ne desire thy neyghboures wyfe ne godes thus charite fulfyllyng goddes loue endynge gode werkys charite pacient benigne hath noon enuye worcheth shrewedenesse loueth nat pryde couetyth worldly worshippes secheth noo propre godes nat wrothe thynketh noon euyll ioyeth nat wyckydnesse trouthe taketh thynge mekely byleuyth god sayth hopyth blys suffreth harmes neuir dis onforted goddes helpe abyde longe falleth neuyr downe worlde ne kepyth man byleue maketh hym stable vnder hym waxith obedyence pacience ouircomyth wronges without man plesyth god man peryssheth therfore ayenste enuye sekythe charite gret study thou maist haue thy lyuynge dwell perfitely therin thyn endyng pthe thrid synne wrathe whiche wycked sterynge mane hert wherby wyl auege hym selue vpon euyn cristen cometh many shreude spice fighting chydynge hurtyng betynge grudchyng wa ieng cursynge cruelnes slaughter desiryng vengeaunce ther also foure speciall one whan thou art sone meuyd sone swaged easy nother whanne thou arte nat sone swagyd shrewyd thridde whanne thou arte sone meuyd nat sone swagyd perilous fourthe longe thou meuyd sone swagyd mooste easy therfore ayenst thies bra ches thou muste arme vertue pacience thynke peyn sorowe might fall thy wordes dedys thenne put cristes passion peynes bitwene suche peynes myght suffre shal thy wrathe sone slake foure thynges spirytually necessarye haue pacience one ayenst thyn ennemye nodre cruell thou nedyst pacience soft speche slaketh wrach therfore aduersite fall suffre paciently whether thou haue deseruyd nat thou haue deseruyd thou arte worthy thou haue thou haste thy rewarde cryste whan sayth blessyd pacient shall called child god nother whanne thy souerayne correctith thy defautes thou muste pacient drawe thy horne pryde snayll whanne touched dyd adam voyce oure lorde tye thridde losse thy good ioob whanne grugest thou steryst god agenst sayth isodre pthe fourthe synne couetyse whiche wrong desyre yt man hath haue thing haue right therto stondith two thyngys pryncipally one whan thou wrongfully purchasist getyst ony maner thynge sacrylege symony stelthe vsury ony falsehede gyle worldy men vse whiche cast alle theyr besynesse soo couetyse ne recke come good soo haue synne gylty yt mony pthe syxte despyte dysobedyence yt thou doost thy moder holy chyrche forbedeth suche play pthe vii fraude desceyte thou doost also thy felowe play viii cursed wreth stryf cometh therof wherby ofte thou reynest god lesyst thy kyndely wytte ix brekyng thy holy day tho dayes vsed x manslaughter ofte fallyth game xi ydolatry thou dost thou makyst ayenst dyce token aboue thy god thyse myscheue many moo comyth sory playe thou wynnest atte playe al thy besines thou hast therwith thou maist reioyse nedys thou must yeue youre yf thou haue hym thou makyst playe strentgh ayenst wyl thou art bound rest fals wytnes pthe ix x whan thou desyrest falsely thy neyghbours wyff ony good thus fals couetyse contraryeth al commaundementis wyll god therfore fle thynke suche fals getyn goodes thou make restytucion amende thou go hen thou shalt hangyd hel ende mammona whiche deuyll couetyse yeueth foure commaundedementis seruauntis one thou kepe well thyn another thou yeue ne doo almes thirde thou etyst drynkest gredely fall tho yt fastyng dayes wyll abyde houre noon sytte lenger mete ete tyme another tyme ofte tyme que che theyr hunger wyth brede spyces ouer moche drynke drede hunger thus breke vygylls ymber dayes frydayes lenten suche another thou castis lyue delytes passyng thyn estate hast noo ioye thou mayst speke suche welfare thynkynge best besette thou spen pdyst theron thou mayst well vse suche deynty metis drinkys synne sayth saint gregore syn nether mete ne drynke appetyte talent delytist soo moche therin thyrd surfete thou pomperist thy body wyth moche mete drink thou mayst brouke lesyst thy syght speche wytte iangelyng bostyng wenyng saye well ayenst reason falle make ryot rere sopers destroye vyteyle yt many poure man myght releuyd fourth curyosite wha thou canst nat holde payed wyth easy fare gadriste many curyous metys encreace thyn appetyte thenne quenche thyn hungre falle waste goodes etyng drynkyng greate festys makyng ayenst thyse cursyd brau chi thou must kepe abstynence metis drynkys thyng dryueth awaye sekenes ne destroyeth lust flesshe thenne doth mesurable takyng mete drynke fyue maner folke ben excused fro fastynge wymmen wyth chyld laborer pylgrymis childre olde folke seke alle thyse synne ete twys daye mesurable susteyne nature theyr appetyte ther dyuerse abstynence also dyuers personys seke absteyneth hym may ete medycyne nedy hath wherof couetous wold spende gloton ete ypocryte holde holy vertuous man deserue mede abstenneth hym bothe excesse mete lust synne thys shold eche man kepe power techeth saint poule whan saith praye straungers pylgrymis ye absteyne flesshely desyres fyght ayenste sowle also destroye body thyse myscheues comyn glotonye ingendryth sorys b gyth sekenes destroyeth vertues dulleth wytte hastyth deth worse maketh lyke beste fuller thy body e tyer thy sowle vertu therfore vse abstynence saith saint aust n thyse vertues shal folowe abstynen sauyth thy mynde sharpeth thy wytte clensyth thy sowle dressyth thy yght maketh holy thy fame swagy thy synne makyth strong thy blood norysheth thy mary destroyeth lechery renewyth thy bloode le g yth thyn age pthe syxte synne slowth greuaunce ye goostly dedys spryngeth many shrewd braunches po drawe longe tary good dedes thou sholdest doo whiche myght tourne helthe thy sowle many panother dulnesse heuynesse herte letteth loue god maketh thou haste noo lykyng goddys seruyce though thou praye thyn herte theron thyrd ydelnesse whiche moche vsed lettyth v begynne ony good werkys lyghtly makyth v leue begynne made kynde traueyle synne flowth holdith v ydelnesse ayenste kynde therfore thou wolt sauyd thou must flee ydelnesse enemye crysten sowlis stepmoder goodnes vertues key vyces alwaye doo somme good werkis sayth saynt ierome deuyll fynde purgatory shall scourgyd wyth men hell wyth deuyls wher neuer shall haue rest therfore besy vertu alwaye thynk noo thyng makyth man soo heuy ne soo soone inclyne synne ydelnes seuenth synne lecherye goostely gretter synne myscheuous thenne therin thou dost sacrylege yt saye thou brekest sacramente wedlok wherof ther cometh ofte vnryghtfull heyris fals maryagis synne dowblyth ofte tyme done man maryed woma maryed one thyse four myscheuys folowe customably vse synne one pouerte another lesyng membre thirde perpetuall pryson fourthe sodeyn deth fayleth hardely custumably vsyd sayd afore another incest wyth thy kynne thyn affynyte another thou mysuseste thyn wyf dost ayenst kynde ordre maryage thou mayst slee thy self thin swerde soo thou mayst wyth thyn wyf synne oname iacobys cosin smyten deth seuen husboundis sara also pthis sacrament sholde doon vsed honestely wyth grete reuerence another synneth wyth kynne wyf contrarye right perylous may wedde noon kynne yf maryage nought worse maye knowe wyff noo afterward forme wedlocke wythout dedely synne requyred another fowlest stynkyng whiche synne ayenst kynde deuyll techyth bothe man woman dyuersytes synne soo abhomynable may nempnyd oonely shryfte ben fallen therin greate horryble thy synne auaylyth shryfte soo shame tellyng grete parte thy penaunce synne soo displeysynge god made reyne brymstone fyre dystroyed fyue cytes sodom gomer deuyll hym selff causyth synne hath shame deed thyse many flesshely synnes whyche ben dedely euerychewers thenne comyn oute foule synne lechery whiche well knowen yt lyuen lustis theyr synne wretched wayes thou myght drawe thyse bee thy bodely wyttys thenne take thy ghoostely wyttes mynde vnderstondyng wylle reason immagynacion saye haue minde kyndenesse god thy last ende thou shalt neuer synne vnderstonde also crystis loore techynges lete euer thy wylle redy worshyp god thought word dede wythout ony werynes lete aso also rewle thy dedys ynward outward crystis lore techyng charged forgyue say euery man repentaunt asketh foryeuenesse yet may nat euery preest generally tyme nede auctorite pope busshop right hath power ete hath nat wherof soo prestes power haue power yet muste gyuen theym soueraynes whanne moche shall execute ther may man chese confessoure pope aboue without auctorite elles theym haue power vnder hym nedes muste shreuyn owne curate yet certen cause leue curat may whanne curate lacketh discrecion nother whanne thou chaungest thyn householde art vagabond peryll deth whan thou entryst see greate peryll thou maist also confesse lay man haue clerly purgyd purgatorye may clerely appere sight oure lorde thy contricion greate thy penaunce may lesse lytell thy peynes muste nedes bee greter soo grete may suffiseth thy saluacion satisfaccion diuerse doctoures puttyng away cause syn nat takynge hede suggestiones also obligacion doon god werkes god mekenesse lowenes herte qualyte quantyte thy synne pthis satisfaccion muste wylfully without grudgyng muste plener generall euery synne reasonably pryuy penaunce pryuy synne open penaunce opyn synne thre principall werkys ther satisfacion almes prayer fastynge thre oure lorde fulfylled hys passion redempcion oure synne therfore almes howe sholde doon shall tell almes lowynge thyn hert wylfull compassion nede dede mercy co passion neyghboures myscheyf thre maner almes one contricion thyn hert synne thou offeryst thy selue god nother geuyng bodilye treasoure thyn honde thrid pyte compassion hauyng thy neyghboures myscheyf temporal almes thou maist somtyme yeue godes vntruly goten say whe thou knowest nat whome thou shalt restore yet muste doone counceyll thy goostly fader tythe nat thou getyst thyft tyme chalengyd thene delyuered shall aske ayen somtyme chaunged shall nat askyd agayne whan turneth nat taker bicause come thefte robbrye raueyn symonye vsu ye theym shall noo almes gyuen must restored agayn whanne hauynge chaunged shall nat asked agayn gyftes comen wymen iogelers suche thenne shal gyuen almes also thou fynde thynge value tyme thou haste doon thy besynes wy e duly owyd thou shalt sped almes counceyll thy gostlye fader haue nede also thou shalt gyue thyn almes gode badde frende ennemye thou power oure lorde sayth yeue euery man asketh turn nat awaye thy face pore sayth toby yet saide yeue gode man resceyue nat synner yt say gyue nature susteyned nat synne norisshed thou norysshest synne yeuest thy gode iougelers iapers suche yt loue ydell suffrest poure man haue hungre myscheyf suche maner geuynge forboden pyte sayth saint ambrose shall nat swete moche plentouous muste thenne good vertuous lyuynge thou shalt rather gyue thy kynne neyghboure theyr nede vertuous thou shalt also yeue olde men wymen chylde haue nede rather thenne theym fall grete pouerte pouert falleth nat ryot array pompe world yet rather gyue thenne pore vnseruyd opyn thyn hert theym aske loue gode withoute difficultye gyue charyte gode wyll elles thou makest nat due satisfactyon thy synne also glade chere meke spyryte soo thou vayn glorye ne spyse natt poure man thou art yeue hastely tary nat fro yt suffreth aguysshe sayth salamo pyeue also discrescion thou haue moche yeue moche thou haue lytell yeue lytell gladly sayeth thoby thus bodily goostly euery body may yeue almes pfurthermore ayenst concupiscence thy flesshe thou haste fastyng hard goynge lyuynge bytter wepynge knockyng thy breest knelynge sharpe disciplyne roddes thyn owne hondes trauayll pylgramage tribulaciones anguyssh sekenesse suche bodily disease paciently suffred scourge god suche penaunce wylfully taken discrete confessoure wyll put parte thy satisfaction penaunce fastynge wylfull abstinence fro mete drynke wherby thy synne wasshen thy flessh made lowe desire euirlastynge blysse gostly fastyng fro bodily syn temporall ioye saint iherom sayth profyteth natt feble thy body fastynge whanne thy herte swelleth pryde somme faste sekenesse may nat ete somme pouerte som ypocrysye somme worshyp god thou must modre thy fastynge thy stomake nat greuyd moche excesse lytell mete mesurably tempreth proufytteth body soul disposeth goostly trauayll ther ete moo delicate mete whenne faste thenne doo ii melys whanne faste nat maner breke faste also prayer ayenst pryde two maner one inwarde thy soull withoute shewynge voyce nother also ordeyned thre party satisfaction ayenst pryde prayer louynge desire thy soull god speche mouthe gaderyng wordes aske good god vttering thy voyce pof foure frutefull prayer saynte poul speketh whenne sayth pray first thynge ther obsecraciones orisones postulaciones yeldyng thankynges obsecraciones whenne thou seest thy soul multitude synne lytell thy merytes seest horryble peynes hell thou maist nat voyde thyn owne vertue ne darst nat thyn owne vnworthynes make thy prayer thy selue makest supplicacons menys thou sayst sanctum maria os pro nobis oure lorde thy passion delyuer v orison whanne thou hast forsaken thy synne askest foryeuenes open speche postulacion whanne thy penaunce doon thou haste sad hope foryeuenes thou pray also thynge ayenst thyn owne spede poull prayed temptacion myght putte away oure lord wyll nat graunte thynges thou mayst pray condicion thynges without condicion haue grace blys oure lorde thou mayst aske without co dicion saynt bernard sayth thou maist aske lord grace godenesse please hym lyue see blysse able thy self vertues worshyp withouten ende pyet afore prayer thou must make redy thy soull dyuerse wyse firste thou must withdrawe thyn hert fro outwarde besynesse beynge wyl kepe thy thoughtes thy first entent thou muste considre also vnworthy thou arte prayest howe worthy thou prayest vnto howe greate thy synnes thou prayest thou muste also clene soull thy prayer shorte let doon stedfaste hope shorte prayer sad hope feithfully doon acceptable god longe prayer fayntly doon withoute hope yet theym occupyed dyuyne seruyce longe prayer spedefull pray also voys spedefull thanne thynke whysper grisostum sayth thus thou loude voyce prayest whysperyst thou suffryst noon praye aboute therfore thy synne thy payn encreased wyttyngly thy self nat herd god must also doon without interupcion nat say nowe verse pater noster bitwene iangle tel tale withoute greate nede ne haste moche thou must also make comon place tyme persones paull sayth wyll men pray euery place yet church principally oure lorde sayth house shal called house praier tymes tymes prayer yet holy church seuen oures ordeyned tyme prayer whiche moste specialy longeth religiouse men oure lord afore passion traueyled nyght prayer oure lady ioseph also rose euery nyght mydnyght saide psalmes commendacion dyd dauid householde though may nat thus yse theym bou de haue noo lettynge must also made w ith nat alwaye allone acceptable god pleasaunt aungelles confusion deuyll thou makest nother bettre thou makest thy selue pand though oure lorde nat anone thy prayer thy wyll yet heryth graunteth happely spedefull thynge longe desired last comyth deynte pit muste also doon deuocyon deuocion clerkes sayn tendernesse herte wherby thou breakyst lightly tearys also wyll loue lyfte vp god heuynly creature uynge inwarde outewarde seruyce god suche deuocion purgeth bothe body soull pand thus deuocion may knowen two pryncipall token one gretenesse voyce outwarde grete fyre knowen flame nother terys righte fyre dryueth oute moysture fro wete wode soo deuocion bringeth oute tearys thyn eyn prayer pwele hath suche plentye tearys disposed grace somme haue greate plentye tearys fro daye daye prayer deuoutly redynge spekynge yet wyll nat leue synne ne trauayll withstonde temptacions ne knowe ne kepe preceptes oure lorde suche teares nat accepte due sacrifyce bifore oure lorde thou full contryte sayth aldrede trusteste mercy god confessed wyll thy penaunce nat wyll turne ageyn thy synne thenne saith suche teares please god wasshe awaye thy synnes turment deuyll sayth saynt bernarde thenne kyndes turmentes may doo sithen deuocion muste euery prayer yet tyme therof shulde principally vsed tyme masse foure cause oone presence oure lorde god nat onlye godhode also manhode tooke loue mannys soull secounde multitude aungelles ther euermore present yelde worshyp almyghty god thrydde grete profyt spede body soull haue vertue sacrament bothe theym present specially theym worthely mynde reason wyll mynde sholde reste god reason thou shold knowe god wyll thou sholde loue god synne thy mynde vnstable thy reson blynde thy wyll croked thou forsakest thy god pthe reformacion therfore thy mynde brynge agayn thy hert trauayled veyn thoughtes prayer redynge often thynkynge god incarnacion passion innumerable benefetys gracious yeftes hauyng grete sorowe thy greate vnkyndnesse yt thou alway shewedyst reformacion thy reason byleue sadly fayth holy churche oure lorde oure greate comforte hath yeuen v knowlege scripture may fynde necessary spedefull oure soull hele nat folowe therin oure naturall wyll submytte oure wytte rule feyth vnderstondyng holy doctoures soo gostly clensed sacrament penaunce reformacion thy wyll also withstode vyces gode wyll truly feythfully encreace abyde vertues god without curiosite wyll double desyre ne none affeccion plesynge butt suche accordynge wyll god pthus cosidred worthynesse thy soull horroure thy synne wherwith thy soul thus wounded take salue penaunce thre plaster contricion cofession satisfaccion bynde sadly thy sore bondes hope drede hope haue foryeuenes thy synne hope grace lyue well hope glorye withoute ende reigne perpetually heuyns blysse drede also peynes hell thou dispayre mercy hym propre haue mercy spare soo euery synne saith saint austyn ther absolucion neuir greate myght greter worse thenne destrouble tho blood drawe man woma vyolence vylony make drawen chirch churcheyerde wherfore churche churcheyerd enterdited suspe tho ayenst ryght oure lorde kynge also thein susteyne warre ageynst kynge wrongfully tho yt comune robber e mansleers hem self defendynge tho ayenst greate char e kyng cofermyd court rome al tho fals wytnes bere wrongely namely cause matrymonye courte oute courte tho false wytnes brynge forthe right matrymony destrouble man woman disherite man la de tenement catel false aduocates mede put forth fals excepciones querels whiche right matrymonye fordoon maner right stede iugement tho mede fauour encheson malicyously man woman brynge oute good fame wycked make theym lese worldly godes honoure putte theym wrongfully purgacio ame bifore tho maliciously distroble lett right presentment churche ther patrone sholde presente therto procoure word dede false enqueste power tho maliciously despysen maundmet kynge take cursed man fro tyme yt hath leyn cursyng xl day remedye wyll seke tho capcions distrouble wyth false iugement false enqueste tho lyueraunce purcha e ayenst right holy church tho e take distroble pea ther loue sholde charite stryf mayntene worde dede tyll haue yelden agayn mede toke theym may neuyr assoyled tho hold house maners graunges persones vycares man hooly churche ayenst wyll attourneys wyll tho maner godes meuable vnmeuable awaye bere strength wrongefully awaye drawe wasten whiche synge may nat assoiled tyll haue made satisfaccion wronge doone tho maner godes violence e bere oute holy churche stedde bbey house religyon whiche therin leyde doon warandise socour kepe therto procour tho theym mayntene susteyne al tho haue leyde hond preest clerke malyce butt selue defendynge tho counceyll helpe ayenst cristendome child wrongfully fader wyttyngly ther child wyten man malice tho werye sle generaciones child distroye drynkes crafte tho false money make therto assent tho good money clyppe shere auantage disceyue al tho yt false pope bulles kynges sea tho bye sell fals mesures false weyghtes say bye one sell nother tho false kynges standarde self wyttynge tho testament distrouble therto procoure word dede wherfore dedys wyll nat fulfilled tho forswere hem self vpon holydome wyllynge wetyngly mede hate doo man woman lese ther worldly godes honoure rubber reuers openly preuely daye nyghte mannys goodes stele wherfore worthy haue iugement tho witholde mannys goode hath spyred thryse hooly churche theym selue wyttyng tho distrouble pea holy churche londe kinges felones tho yt mayntene false conspiratoures false forswerers assy e courte tho fals pleyntes putte forth ageynst fraunchise holychurche kinge royalme tho offrynges offred holy churche churcheyerde chapel oratory stede prouynce caunterbury
